var url = 'https://location.nhk.or.jp/geoip/area.json'
fetch(url)
  .then((response) => response.json())
  .then((data) => {
    if (data.is_gdpr_state) {
      var cookieDomain = _satellite.getVar("cookieDomain");
      var orga = '02C51F6A550AFE4E0A4C98A7%40AdobeOrg';
      var optoutCookies = [{key:'AAoptout',value:'true'},{key:'cb_optout',value:'1'},{key:'CBoptout',value:'true'},{key:'SSoptout',value:'true'}];
      // ADOBE_WG-2695：s_ppv_noll も不要なCookieであると判明しているが、Cookieを保持している訪問者を考慮し、余裕を持って2024年11月ごろに対象から除外予定
      var removeCookies = [`AMCV_${orga}`,`AMCVS_${orga}`, 's_ecid','s_cc','s_sq','s_catvwd_nol','s_ppv_nol','s_ips_nol','s_tp_nol','s_ppv_noll','s_nr_nol'];

      if (window._satellite) {
        optoutCookies.forEach(e => _satellite.cookie.set(e.key, e.value, {domain: cookieDomain, sameSite: "none", secure: true, expires: 365*10, path: '/'}));
        removeCookies.forEach(e => document.cookie = `${e}=0;SameSite=None;Secure;max-age=0;Path=/;domain=${cookieDomain};`);
      } else if (window.s_Obj) {
        optoutCookies.forEach(e =>  s_Obj.c_w(e.key, e.value));
        removeCookies.forEach(e => s_Obj.c_w(e, "", new Date(1000)));
      }
    } else {
      adobe.optIn.approveAll();
      adobe.optIn.complete();
    }
});
});

/**
 * tc main processing.
 * @param : none
 */
function _tc_main() {
	// initial processing
	try {
		_tc_init();
	} catch (e) {
	}
	// try {
	// 	_tc_sc_execute();
	// } catch (e) {
	// }
}

/**
 * initial processing.
 * @param : none
 */
function _tc_init() {  
	_tc_createCustomParam();
}

/**
 * create custom object.
 * @param : none
 */
function _tc_createCustomParam() {
	_tc_info = new _tc_initInfo();  
	_tc_createConObject();
	_tc_setEventVars();
}

/**
 * create container.
 * @param : none
 */
function _tc_createConObject() {
	if (typeof (_tc_container01) !== 'undefined') {
		_tc_con.c1 = _tc_container01;
	} else if (typeof (_ga_container01) !== 'undefined') {
		_tc_con.c1 = _ga_container01;
	} else {
		_tc_con.c1 = _tc_notval;
	}

	if (typeof (_tc_container02) !== 'undefined') {
		_tc_con.c2 = _tc_container02;
	} else if (typeof (_ga_container02) !== 'undefined') {
		_tc_con.c2 = _ga_container02;
	} else {
		_tc_con.c2 = _tc_notval;
	}

	if (typeof (_tc_container03) !== 'undefined') {
		_tc_con.c3 = _tc_container03;
	} else if (typeof (_ga_container03) !== 'undefined') {
		_tc_con.c3 = _ga_container03;
	} else {
		_tc_con.c3 = _tc_notval;
	}

	if (typeof (_tc_container04) !== 'undefined') {
		_tc_con.c4 = _tc_container04;
	} else if (typeof (_ga_container04) !== 'undefined') {
		_tc_con.c4 = _ga_container04;
	} else {
		_tc_con.c4 = _tc_notval;
	}

	if (typeof (_tc_container05) !== 'undefined') {
		_tc_con.c5 = _tc_container05;
	} else if (typeof (_ga_container05) !== 'undefined') {
		_tc_con.c5 = _ga_container05;
	} else {
		_tc_con.c5 = _tc_notval;
	}

	for (var i = 1; i < _TC_CUSTOM_VARIABLE_COUNT + 1; i++) {
		var keyname_tc_containers = 'container' + ('00' + i).slice(-2);
		var keyname_tc_con_c = 'c' + i;
		var keyname_tc_con_ce = 'ce' + i;
		if ((typeof (_tc_containers) !== 'undefined') && (typeof (_tc_containers[keyname_tc_containers]) !== 'undefined')) {
			_tc_con[keyname_tc_con_c] = _tc_containers[keyname_tc_containers];
		} else if (typeof (_tc_con[keyname_tc_con_c]) == 'undefined') {
			_tc_con[keyname_tc_con_c] = _tc_notval;
		}
		_tc_con[keyname_tc_con_ce] = _tc_con[keyname_tc_con_c];
	}
}

/**
 * set custom event variables.
 * @param : none
 */
function _tc_setEventVars() {
	if (typeof (_tc_form_events) != 'undefined') {
		var validEvents = _tc_getValidEvents(_tc_form_events);
		if (typeof (validEvents) != 'undefined'
			&& validEvents instanceof Array
			&& validEvents.length == 2
			&& validEvents[0]
			&& validEvents[1]) {

			_tc_eventVars.events = validEvents[0];
		}
	}
}

/**
 *	Function that users can bind with a click event of link, button, etc.
 *	@sc_obj : Adobe Analytics object
 *	@aavars : key:value pairs the user want to send to Adobe Analytics
 *	@linkName : the name of link clicked
 *  Since 2015/01/15
 */
function _tc_onClick(a, b, c) {
    if (!a) {
        return
    }
    a.linkTrackVars = _tc_aa_notval;
    a.linkTrackEvents = _tc_aa_notval;
    for (var i = 1; i < _TC_CUSTOM_VARIABLE_COUNT + 1; i++) {
        var d = 'c' + i;
        var f = 'ce' + i;
        _tc_con[d] = null;
        _tc_con[f] = _tc_notval
    }
    _tc_eventVars.events = '';
    try {
        a.linkTrackVars = 'eVar4,eVar5,eVar6,eVar7,eVar8,eVar9,eVar12,eVar13,eVar14,eVar15,eVar29,' + 'eVar39,eVar40,eVar84,prop12,prop35,prop36,prop37,prop38,prop42,events,' + _tc_getEvars();
        a.linkTrackEvents = 'event12';
        _tc_eventVars.events = 'event12';
        for (var g in b) {
            try {
                if (g == 'events') {
                    var h = b[g];
                    var j = _tc_getValidEvents(h);
                    if (typeof (j) != 'undefined' && j && j instanceof Array && j.length == 2 && j[0] && j[1]) {
                        a.linkTrackEvents = a.linkTrackEvents + "," + j[1];
                        _tc_eventVars.events = _tc_eventVars.events + "," + j[0]
                    }
                    continue
                }
                var k = g.substring(0, 4);
                if (k == 'prop') {
                    var l = g.substring(4, g.length);
                    if (isNaN(l)) {
                        continue
                    }
                    var m = parseInt(l);
                    if (m < _TC_CUSTOM_PROP_MIN || _TC_CUSTOM_PROP_MAX < m) {
                        conitnue
                    }
                    var h = b[g];
                    if (typeof (h) == 'undefined' || !h) {
                        continue
                    }
                    a.linkTrackVars = a.linkTrackVars + "," + g;
                    var n = _TC_MY_CUSTOM_PROP_MIN + (m - _TC_CUSTOM_PROP_MIN);
                    _tc_con['c' + n] = h;
                    continue
                }
                if (k == 'eVar') {
                    var l = g.substring(4, g.length);
                    if (isNaN(l)) {
                        continue
                    }
                    var m = parseInt(l);
                    if (m < _TC_CUSTOM_EVAR_MIN || _TC_CUSTOM_EVAR_MAX < m) {
                        conitnue
                    }
                    var h = b[g];
                    if (typeof (h) == 'undefined' || !h) {
                        continue
                    }
                    var o = _TC_MY_CUSTOM_EVAR_MIN + (m - _TC_CUSTOM_EVAR_MIN);
                    _tc_con['ce' + o] = h;
                    continue
                }
            } catch (e) {}
        }
          var p = (c) ? c : _tc_aa_notval;
        a.eVar9 = 'D=pageName';
        a.eVar12 = _tc_getMeasurementId(p);
        a.prop12 = _tc_getMeasurementId(p);
        a.eVar84 = '_tc_onClick';

        // ADOBE_WG-2967 START
        if (/^\/archives\//.test(location.pathname)) {
          var body = document.querySelector("body");
          var dataGenre = body.getAttribute("data-genre");
          if (/\/movies\/.*/.test(location.pathname) || (/\/articles\/.*/.test(location.pathname)) && dataGenre === "jinbutsu") {
            _satellite.logger.log("DAS-ID");
            // DAS-ID
            a.linkTrackVars = a.linkTrackVars + "," + "eVar87";
            a.eVar87 = body.getAttribute("data-id");
          }
          // else if (/\/articles\/.*/.test(location.pathname) && dataGenre !== "jinbutsu") {
            // 記事-ID
            //a.linkTrackVars = a.linkTrackVars + "," + "eVar88";
            //a.eVar88 = body.getAttribute("data-id");
          //}
          a.linkTrackVars = a.linkTrackVars + "," + "eVar89";
          a.eVar89 = dataGenre;
        }
        // ADOBE_WG-2967 END

        a.tl(this, 'o', p);
      　　a.clearVars();
        _satellite.logger.info('Firing custom link beacon by calling _tc_onClick: ' + p)
    } catch (e) {}
}

/**
 *	get  measurement identifier.
 *	@str : string
 *	@return [measurement identifier]string
 *  Since 2015/02/12
 */
function _tc_topDir(str) {

	return _tc_getMeasurementId(str);
}

/**
 *	get  measurement identifier.
 *	@str : string
 *	@return [measurement identifier]string
 *  Since 2017/08/10
 */
function _tc_getMeasurementId(str) {
	var result = null;
	if (typeof (_tc_msid) == 'string' && _tc_msid !== '') {
		var w_topDir = '[' + s_omni.getStrInMaxBytes(_tc_msid, 100) + ']';
	} else {
		if (location.pathname.split('/').length > 2) {
			var w_topDir = '[' + location.pathname.split('/')[1] + ']';
		} else {
            if (location.pathname.match("^\/$|^\/index\.html$")) {
                var w_topDir = '[top]';
            } else {
                var w_topDir = "";
            }
		}
	}
	result = w_topDir + str;

	return result;
}

/**
 *	select only valid events from a list
 *	@sEvents : comma separated string of event names (including valid and invalid)
 *	@return : another comma separated string of only valid event names
 *  Since 2015/01/15
 */
function _tc_getValidEvents(sEvents) {
	var ret = new Array();
	if (typeof (sEvents) == 'undefined') {
		return ret;
	}
	if (!sEvents) {
		return ret;
	}
	var newArr = new Array();
	var keyArr = new Array();
	var items = sEvents.split(',');
	var len = items.length;
	for (var i = 0; i < len; ++i) {
		try {
			var item = items[i];
			var head = item.substring(0, 5);
			if (head != 'event') {
				continue;
			}
			var equalIndex = item.indexOf('=');
			if (equalIndex == -1) {
				equalIndex = item.length;
			}
			var tail = item.substring(5, equalIndex);
			if (isNaN(tail)) {
				continue;
			}
			var num = parseInt(tail);
			if (num < _TC_CUSTOM_EVENT_MIN || _TC_CUSTOM_EVENT_MAX < num) {
				continue;
			}
			if (equalIndex != item.length) {
				var cnt = item.substring(equalIndex + 1, item.length);
				if (isNaN(cnt)) {
					continue;
				}
			}
			keyArr.push(head + tail);
			newArr.push(item);
		} catch (e) {
		}
	}
	ret.push(newArr.join(','));
	ret.push(keyArr.join(','));
	return ret;
}

/**
 *	return eVar56～eVar75
 *  @param : none
 *  @return : [Variable name of eVar56～eVar75]string
 *	Since 2017/01/05
 */
// _tc_onClickで使用されているためそのままにする（上書きして制御している可能性もあるので）  
function _tc_getEvars() {
	var evars = 'eVar56,eVar57,eVar58,eVar59,eVar60,eVar61,eVar62,eVar63,eVar64,eVar65';
	return evars;
}

/**
 *	initialize _tc_info
 *  @param : none
 *	Since 2017/01/05
 */
function _tc_initInfo() {
	// var canonicalURL = undefined;
	var canonicalURL = _satellite.getVar("getCanonicalURL") || undefined;

	// var sdrVer = '7.2.3';  // SDR version.
	var sdrVer = _satellite.getVar("getSDRver") || '7.2.3';  // SDR version.

	// var parentURL;
	var parentURL = _satellite.getVar("getParentURL") || undefined;

	// new function () {
	// 	try {
	// 		var links = document.getElementsByTagName("link");
	// 		for (var i = 0; i < links.length; i++) {
	// 			if (links[i].rel) {
	// 				if (links[i].rel.toLowerCase() == "canonical") {
	// 					canonicalURL = links[i].href;
	// 				}
	// 			}
	// 		}
	// 	} catch (e) {
	// 	}
	// 	try {
	// 		try {
	// 			var p_url = window.parent.location.href;
	// 			if ((typeof (p_url) == 'undefined') || (p_url == '')) {
	// 				p_url = document.referrer;
	// 			}
	// 		} catch (e) {
	// 			var p_url = document.referrer;
	// 		}
	// 		var c_url = window.location.href;
	// 		if (p_url == c_url) {
	// 			parentURL = 'N/A';
	// 		} else {
	// 			parentURL = p_url;
	// 		}
	// 	} catch (e) {
	// 		parentURL = 'ERR';
	// 	}
	// };
	this.getCanonicalURL = function () {
		try {
			if (typeof (canonicalURL) !== 'undefined') {
				return canonicalURL;
			} else {
				return null;
			}
		} catch (e) {
			return null;
		}
	};

	this.getSDRver = function () {
		try {
			if (typeof (sdrVer) !== 'undefined') {
				return sdrVer;
			} else {
				return null;
			}
		} catch (e) {
			return null;
		}
	};

	this.getParentURL = function () {
		return parentURL;
	};

}

/**
 *	Function that users can bind with a update page event without loading.
 *  @sc_obj : Adobe Analytics object
 *  @return : none
 *	Since 2019/02/04
 */
function _tc_updatePage(sc_obj) {
	if (!sc_obj) {
		return;
	}

	try {
		sc_obj.clearVars();
		_tc_eventVars.events = '';
		if ((typeof (_tc_va_nowPlayingFlag) !== 'undefined') && (_tc_va_nowPlayingFlag == true)) {
			sc_obj.contextData = new Object();
		}

		_tc_init();
		sc_obj.t();
      	sc_obj.clearVars();
	} catch (e) {
		return true;
	}
}
